# Real-Fit Adapter Smoke

## Objective

Fit a synthetic-real-like A2 dataset with `RealDataFitter.to_full_config()`, regenerate through the A3 fitted-config adapter, and compare spectra.

## Command

`PYTHONPATH=bench/nirs_synthetic_pfn/src python bench/nirs_synthetic_pfn/experiments/exp00_real_fit_adapter.py --n-samples 96 --source-seed 20260429 --regen-seed 20260430`

## Config

- Samples: 96
- Source seed: 20260429
- Regeneration seed: 20260430
- Source preset: agriculture grain, FOSS XDS, reflectance, regression target
- Fitted-only gate variant: `fitted_instrument`

- Return code: 0
- Entries: 6
- Status counts: `{'??': 5, 'M': 1}`

## Candidate Mapping Diagnostics

| area | status | gate eligible | finding |
|---|---|---|---|
| `n_components` | `passed` | `False` | Fitted component fill to n_components=6 used `['starch', 'protein', 'moisture', 'lipid', 'cellulose', 'gluten']` and scientific_status=`failed`; failed metrics=`correlation_length, derivative_statistics, peak_density, baseline_curvature`. This uses only fitted_config.domain and fitted_config.n_components, but it imputes component identities that RealDataFitter did not detect, so it remains diagnostic. |
| `boundary_components_config` | `not_applicable` | `False` | Actual fitted boundary_components_config is empty for this source; no fitted-only boundary component can be executed. Non-empty configs remain diagnostic until the bench adapter has an exact ComponentLibrary mapping for fitted band_center/bandwidth/amplitude. |
| `baseline_curvature` | `blocked` | `False` | RealDataFitter exposes aggregate final-spectrum baseline and edge-curvature indicators, but not an inverse mapping to generator polynomial baseline coefficients. The fitted residual-effects contract now executes observed-spectrum baseline coefficient distributions separately; any remaining curvature gap needs a source-free residual basis improvement, not source provenance or threshold changes. |
| `preprocessing` | `not_applicable` | `False` | The fitted source is raw_absorbance and is_preprocessed=False; derivative-statistic mismatch is therefore not explained by an executable preprocessing inverse. |

## Final Unblock Memo

No blocker remains: the fitted-only executable contract and scorecard both passed.

## Assumptions

- A3 smoke uses a solid matrix because to_full_config() does not expose matrix_type.
- A3 smoke uses a component-concentration regression target because fitted spectra do not carry y.
- A1 nuisance particle_size uses a range-safe placeholder during canonicalization; fitted particle_size_config.mean_size_um is calibrated against the assumed matrix range later in the A3 builder_config.
- A3 fitted-only maps RealDataFitter nuisance/effect estimates through calibrated generator controls because to_full_config() estimates final-spectrum variability, not raw operator parameters.
- A3 reports raw and effective fitted nuisance/effect controls in builder_config and metadata.
- A3 applies fitted_residual_effects_config additively from observed-spectrum coefficient distributions; no observed residual row is replayed.
